My Review of the Audit
✅ What is solid
You already have:

lifecycle + idempotency framework

lineage contract

quantization policy

append-only + RLS pattern

AuditWriter discipline

The audit correctly identified the real risks — not generic ones.

The Three Critical Clarifications Required
These must be locked before implementation:

1️⃣ Custom Amortization Pattern Contract
This is the biggest risk.

You must define:

Allowed pattern types:
Choose and freeze:

STRAIGHT_LINE

PERCENT_PER_PERIOD

AMOUNT_PER_PERIOD

WEIGHTED_FACTORS

You cannot allow arbitrary free-form arrays without validation rules.

Required invariants:
Total amortized = prepaid amount (within rounding tolerance)

Pattern periods must be sequential and gap-free

No negative amortization unless explicitly allowed

Percent patterns must sum to 100%

Amount patterns must sum to prepaid amount

Weighted factors must normalize deterministically

If you do not freeze this now, schedule regeneration and idempotency will break later.

2️⃣ Supersession & Idempotency Model
This is equally critical.

You must answer:

When schedule is regenerated due to:

adjustment

correction

FX basis change

pattern update

Do we:

A) create new schedule rows with supersedes_id
or
B) use schedule_version_token
or
C) link by schedule_generation_id

Pick one.

My recommendation:

Always append new rows

Use supersedes_id to chain previous rows

Never update schedule rows in-place

Run-level request_signature prevents duplicate runs

If this is not decided now, you will regret it later.

3️⃣ FX Treatment Policy
You must freeze:

Prepaid amortization uses:

month-end selected rate (default)

daily selected rate only if policy = TRANSACTION_DATE_BASIS

no direct fx_rate_quotes access

rate_date persisted per schedule line

This must be deterministic and policy-coded.

Otherwise future reconciliation will be impossible.

What Is NOT a Blocker
These are manageable during implementation:

drill endpoints

workflow structure

API wiring

quota hooks

RLS

The architecture supports these cleanly.

My Final Position
Status:
Prepaid = design clarification required before implementation

You should NOT start coding until:

amortization pattern schema is frozen

supersession chain model is frozen

FX rule is frozen

A) Frozen Amortization Pattern Schema

{
  "type": "object",
  "required": [
    "pattern_type",
    "term_start_date",
    "term_end_date",
    "base_amount_contract_currency",
    "period_frequency"
  ],
  "properties": {
    "pattern_type": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": [
        "straight_line",
        "weighted_period",
        "explicit_percentages",
        "explicit_amounts"
      ]
    },
    "term_start_date": { "type": "string", "format": "date" },
    "term_end_date": { "type": "string", "format": "date" },
    "period_frequency": { "type": "string", "enum": ["monthly"] },
    "base_amount_contract_currency": { "type": "string" },
    "periods": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "required": [
          "period_seq",
          "period_start_date",
          "period_end_date",
          "recognition_date"
        ],
        "properties": {
          "period_seq": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
          "period_start_date": { "type": "string", "format": "date" },
          "period_end_date": { "type": "string", "format": "date" },
          "recognition_date": { "type": "string", "format": "date" },
          "weight": { "type": "string" },
          "percentage": { "type": "string" },
          "amount": { "type": "string" }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
Frozen validation invariants:

term_end_date >= term_start_date.
period_frequency fixed to monthly in 1D.4 core.
periods required for weighted_period, explicit_percentages, explicit_amounts; forbidden for straight_line.
period_seq unique, contiguous 1..N.
Period ranges must be non-overlapping, contiguous, and fully inside term.
recognition_date must be inside its period.
weighted_period: all weight > 0, no percentage/amount.
explicit_percentages: all percentage >= 0, sum of 6dp-quantized percentages must equal exactly 1.000000, no weight/amount.
explicit_amounts: all amount >= 0, sum of 6dp-quantized amounts must equal exactly base_amount_contract_currency (6dp), no weight/percentage.
straight_line: engine-generated periods only, deterministic month grid from term.
Run-signature canonicalization: pattern must be normalized before hashing, with periods sorted by period_seq, numeric fields quantized to 6dp string form, then serialized canonically.
B) Frozen Supersession / Idempotency Strategy

prepaid_amortization_schedule uses schedule_version_token (required), no supersedes_id on schedule rows.
prepaid_adjustments carries the supersession chain using:
supersedes_id (self-reference, append-only chain).
prior_schedule_version_token and new_schedule_version_token.
schedule_version_token generation rule:
SHA256(prepaid_id + pattern_normalized_json + reporting_currency + rate_mode + adjustment_effective_date + prior_schedule_version_token_or_root).
Idempotency constraints:
Unique (run_id, prepaid_id, amortization_date, schedule_version_token).
Unique (run_id, prepaid_id, period_seq, schedule_version_token).
Adjustment idempotency unique (run_id, prepaid_id, effective_date, adjustment_type, idempotency_key).
Regeneration behavior:
Never update old schedule rows.
New version rows inserted with new schedule_version_token.
Effective version for results/drill = latest adjustment chain node for prepaid in run (deterministic order: effective_date desc, created_at desc, id desc), else root token.
C) Frozen FX Policy

Default rate_mode: month_end_locked.
Allowed override: daily_selected only when tenant policy explicitly allows transaction-date basis.
FX source: selected-rate service only (no raw provider table reads in prepaid logic).
Persist per schedule row:
fx_rate_used (6dp),
fx_rate_date,
fx_rate_source (manual_monthly, locked_selection, provider_consensus, previous_valid_selected_rate, same_currency_1_0).
rate_date rule:
month_end_locked: month-end date of amortization period.
daily_selected: recognition_date.
Same-currency: fx_rate_used = 1.000000, fx_rate_date = recognition_date.
Month-end lock enforcement:
If rate_mode=month_end_locked, a locked monthly selection must exist for pair/period.
No fallback to non-locked source when locked mode is required.
Missing lock is hard failure and must append failed run event (error_code: MISSING_LOCKED_RATE).
D) Explicit Invariants List

Prepaid module remains separate from revenue/lease/FAR/consolidation logic.
All writes via AuditWriter; no direct unmanaged writes.
Tenant-scoped tables use RLS ENABLE + FORCE.
Material prepaid tables are append-only (DB trigger-enforced).
Run headers immutable; run state derived from append-only events.
Deterministic request-signature and event idempotency enforced.
Pattern JSON must normalize before signature and before schedule generation.
Schedule supersession is version-token based; no in-place mutation.
Adjustment chain is explicit and append-only via supersedes_id.
FX uses selected-rate abstraction only.
Month-end locked mode fails closed when locked rate absent.
Quantization policy is centralized: rates 6dp, persisted amounts 6dp, output 2dp.
Journal references use PPD- namespace and deterministic sequence.
Rounding residual assigned deterministically to anchor row to prevent drift.
Drill path must be complete: journal/schedule -> prepaid -> source artifact.
Lineage completeness gate must pass before terminal completed event.
Control-plane token/module enablement/RBAC/quota/routing must pass before execution.
E) Implementation-Safe Confirmation

Yes, implementation-safe if the above contracts are treated as locked and reflected in schema constraints, service validation, workflow idempotency checks, and tests.
No unresolved architectural ambiguity remains for 1D.4 core after this freeze.

=======================================================

=======================================================
FROZEN DESIGN CONTRACTS TO IMPLEMENT
=======================================================

A. AMORTIZATION PATTERN TYPES
Allowed pattern types only:
- straight_line
- weighted_period
- explicit_percentages
- explicit_amounts

Pattern schema rules:
- period_frequency fixed to monthly in 1D.4 core
- periods required for weighted_period, explicit_percentages, explicit_amounts
- periods forbidden for straight_line
- period_seq unique and contiguous 1..N
- period ranges non-overlapping, contiguous, fully inside term
- recognition_date inside its period
- weighted_period: weight only, all > 0
- explicit_percentages: percentage only, all >= 0, sum exactly 1.000000 after 6dp quantization
- explicit_amounts: amount only, all >= 0, sum exactly base amount after 6dp quantization
- straight_line: engine-generated month grid only

Run-signature canonicalization:
- periods sorted by period_seq
- numeric fields quantized to 6dp string form
- canonical serialization before hashing

B. SUPERSESSION / IDEMPOTENCY
- prepaid_amortization_schedule uses required schedule_version_token
- no supersedes_id on schedule rows
- prepaid_adjustments uses supersedes_id chain plus:
  - prior_schedule_version_token
  - new_schedule_version_token

schedule_version_token generation:
SHA256(prepaid_id + pattern_normalized_json + reporting_currency + rate_mode + adjustment_effective_date + prior_schedule_version_token_or_root)

Idempotency constraints:
- Unique (run_id, prepaid_id, amortization_date, schedule_version_token)
- Unique (run_id, prepaid_id, period_seq, schedule_version_token)
- Unique (run_id, prepaid_id, effective_date, adjustment_type, idempotency_key) for adjustments

Regeneration rules:
- never update old schedule rows
- new version rows inserted with new schedule_version_token
- effective version resolved deterministically from latest adjustment chain node, else root token

C. FX POLICY
Default rate_mode:
- month_end_locked

Allowed override:
- daily_selected only when tenant policy explicitly allows transaction-date basis

Persist on each schedule row:
- fx_rate_used (6dp)
- fx_rate_date
- fx_rate_source

rate_date rules:
- month_end_locked → month-end date of amortization period
- daily_selected → recognition_date
- same-currency → fx_rate_used = 1.000000 and fx_rate_date = recognition_date

Month-end lock enforcement:
- locked monthly selection must exist when month_end_locked is used
- no fallback to non-locked sources
- missing lock must append failed run event with error_code = MISSING_LOCKED_RATE

=======================================================
PREPAID LOGIC RULES
=======================================================

A. PREPAID REGISTRY
- deterministic prepaid storage only
- no AI extraction
- corrections via append-only superseding rows

B. PATTERN RESOLUTION
- validate frozen schema exactly
- normalize pattern JSON deterministically
- reject unsupported pattern types
- reject invalid sums, overlaps, or gaps

C. SCHEDULE GENERATION
- straight_line → deterministic monthly grid from term
- weighted_period → normalized by weights
- explicit_percentages → exact 6dp percentage allocation
- explicit_amounts → exact 6dp amount allocation
- cumulative amounts must remain deterministic
- rounding residual assigned deterministically to anchor row to prevent drift

D. ADJUSTMENTS / REMEASUREMENT
- append-only only
- no in-place mutation
- generate new schedule_version_token
- create forward-looking regenerated schedule rows
- preserve prior schedule rows
- apply prospective-only unless frozen rule explicitly requires catch-up, using catch_up_amount_reporting_currency where applicable

E. FX INTEGRATION
- selected-rate only
- default month_end_locked
- daily_selected only when tenant policy allows
- same-currency uses 1.000000
- missing month-end lock fails closed

F. JOURNAL PREVIEW
- deterministic preview only, not posting
- use journal namespace helper with PPD- prefix
- every journal row must trace back to schedule row
- drillable lineage required

=======================================================
LINEAGE + DRILLABILITY
=======================================================

Prepaid drill path must support:

amortized expense
→ prepaid_amortization_schedule
→ prepaids
→ source expense snapshot / source artifact

Implement deterministic drill endpoints:

POST /api/v1/prepaid/run
GET /api/v1/prepaid/run/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/prepaid/results/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/prepaid/run/{run_id}/prepaids/{prepaid_id}
GET /api/v1/prepaid/run/{run_id}/schedule-lines/{schedule_id}
GET /api/v1/prepaid/run/{run_id}/journal-entries/{journal_id}

Rules:
- use DrillResponseBase-compatible response shape
- include parent_reference_id
- include source_reference_id
- include correlation_id
- include child_ids
- pure read paths only
- deterministic ordering only

Lineage completeness gate:
Before terminal completed event:
- every schedule line must resolve to prepaid + source expense artifact
- every journal entry must resolve to schedule line
If incomplete:
- append failed event
- error_code = LINEAGE_INCOMPLETE

why full pytest is not produced

Good — this is exactly why we don’t freeze early.

You’re not getting full pytest output because pytest never ran.

It stopped before that.

Let me break it down clearly.

Why full pytest was not produced
From your log:

Execution phase: blocked during alembic upgrade head
Error: migration chain mismatch
KeyError: '0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane'

That means:

scripts/test_all.ps1 runs:

docker up

wait_for_db

alembic upgrade head

THEN pytest

Alembic failed during migration resolution.

Because migration failed, pytest was never executed.

So there is no "full pytest results" because:
👉 the script aborted before reaching pytest.

The Actual Problem
This line is the real issue:

0009_phase1d4_prepaid_core has down_revision = "0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane"
0008 revision id is 0008_phase1e_control_plane
You have a revision ID mismatch.

Alembic doesn’t care about file names.
It cares about the internal revision string inside the migration file.

So what happened?

Most likely:

The filename is 0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane.py

But inside that file, the revision is declared as:

revision = "0008_phase1e_control_plane"
Then in 0009_phase1d4_prepaid_core.py you wrote:

down_revision = "0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane"
But Alembic only sees:

0008_phase1e_control_plane
So it cannot find:

0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane
Hence:

KeyError: '0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane'
This is NOT a logic bug
This is a migration metadata bug.

It is mechanical.

And easy to fix.

What You Must Do
Open:

0008_phase1e_platform_control_plane.py
Check the line:

revision = "..."
Use that exact string as:

down_revision = "..."
inside:

0009_phase1d4_prepaid_core.py
They must match exactly.

No filename guessing.
No assumptions.

Why This Matters
Alembic builds a graph like:

0006 → 0007 → 0008 → 0009
Right now your graph is broken at:

0008 (unknown to 0009)
So migration stops.
So test DB never gets schema.
So pytest never runs.
So full pipeline aborts.

Second Issue: Temporal Failure
You also have:

AttributeError: 'dict' object has no attribute 'event_type'
That is unrelated to migration.

That means:

Somewhere in prepaid finalize activity

You are expecting a typed event object

But you're passing a raw dict

FAR readiness assessment
Platform is ready to implement FAR core as a separate module: run/event scaffolding, AuditWriter path, RLS/append-only patterns, selected-rate FX service, drill schema, Temporal runtime, and control-plane guardrails are already present.
Existing fixed_assets scaffolding is placeholder-only, so there is no conflicting FAR math to unwind.
Readiness level: high, with one naming decision to lock at implementation start: module_code="fixed_assets" (recommended) vs module_code="far".
Required module boundaries
FAR owns only: asset registry, depreciation schedule logic, useful-life/residual policy application, impairment/disposal event handling, FAR journal preview, FAR lineage/drill, FAR workflow orchestration.
FAR must not contain: revenue allocation/recognition rules, lease liability/ROU rules, prepaid amortization patterns, consolidation/elimination logic, raw FX provider handling, control-plane policy authoring.
Reuse only shared infrastructure: accounting_common, AuditWriter, control-plane token checks, selected-rate FX service, async DB/session helpers.
Coupling risks to avoid:
Reusing Prepaid/Lease schedule generators directly (copying business semantics).
Putting FAR-specific formulas into accounting_common.
Reading consolidation outputs as FAR inputs (FAR should use source asset artifacts/snapshots only).
Proposed FAR data model
far_runs
Purpose: immutable logical run header.
Keys: unique (tenant_id, request_signature).
Fields: request_signature, initiated_by, configuration_json, workflow_id, correlation_id.
Governance: append-only, RLS ENABLE+FORCE, AuditWriter-only writes.
far_run_events
Purpose: append-only lifecycle (accepted/running/completed/failed).
Keys: unique (run_id, event_seq), unique (run_id, event_type, idempotency_key).
Fields: event_type, event_time, idempotency_key, metadata_json, correlation_id.
Governance: append-only, RLS ENABLE+FORCE, AuditWriter-only.
assets
Purpose: asset registry + capitalization policy snapshot.
Key strategy: unique (tenant_id, asset_code, created_at) or (tenant_id, asset_code, version_token); corrections via new rows.
Required lineage hooks: source_acquisition_reference, parent_reference_id, source_reference_id, correlation_id.
Supersession: supersedes_id required for registry corrections.
Core fields: asset_code, entity_id, asset_class, asset_currency, reporting_currency, capitalization_date, in_service_date, capitalized_amount_asset_currency, depreciation_method, useful_life_months, residual_value_reporting_currency, rate_mode.
asset_depreciation_schedule
Purpose: deterministic periodic depreciation rows.
Keys: unique (run_id, asset_id, depreciation_date, schedule_version_token) and (run_id, asset_id, period_seq, schedule_version_token).
Lineage hooks: source_acquisition_reference, parent_reference_id, source_reference_id, correlation_id.
Supersession model: no supersedes_id; versioning via schedule_version_token.
FX fields: fx_rate_used, fx_rate_date, fx_rate_source.
asset_impairments
Purpose: append-only impairment events + effect snapshot.
Keys: unique (run_id, asset_id, impairment_date, idempotency_key).
Lineage hooks: required.
Supersession: supersedes_id for correction chain.
Core fields: impairment_date, impairment_amount_reporting_currency, prior_schedule_version_token, new_schedule_version_token, reason.
asset_disposals
Purpose: append-only disposal events + gain/loss components.
Keys: unique (run_id, asset_id, disposal_date, idempotency_key).
Lineage hooks: required.
Supersession: supersedes_id for correction chain.
Core fields: disposal_date, proceeds_reporting_currency, disposal_cost_reporting_currency, carrying_amount_reporting_currency, gain_loss_reporting_currency, prior_schedule_version_token, new_schedule_version_token.
asset_journal_entries
Purpose: deterministic FAR journal preview lines.
Keys: unique (run_id, journal_reference, line_seq).
Traceability: must reference exactly one source row (schedule_id or impairment_id or disposal_id).
Lineage hooks: required.
Governance: append-only, RLS ENABLE+FORCE, AuditWriter-only.
Depreciation design
Supported methods in 1D.5 core:
straight_line (depreciable assets).
non_depreciable (no schedule generation; e.g., land).
Useful life:
Stored as immutable policy snapshot on assets (useful_life_months).
Changes handled via append-only correction/supersession + regenerated schedule version.
Residual value:
Stored per asset in reporting currency.
Hard floor: carrying amount cannot go below residual value.
Frequency and period alignment:
Monthly only in core.
Depreciation date anchored to month-end for full periods.
Partial periods:
Deterministic pro-rata by day count for first/last partial month.
Rounding:
Rate 6dp, persisted amounts 6dp, output 2dp, HALF_UP only.
Residual rounding drift assigned deterministically to final row of each schedule_version_token.
Regeneration:
No updates to old schedule rows.
New forward schedule rows inserted with new schedule_version_token.
Effective version is latest chain node for asset, else root version.
Impairment / disposal design
Impairment event:
Append event row with amount, effective date, reason, idempotency key.
Reduce carrying amount at event date; regenerate future depreciation prospectively with new version token.
Journal preview lines link directly to impairment row.
Disposal event:
Append event row with proceeds/costs/date and idempotency key.
Stop depreciation after disposal effective date.
Compute deterministic gain/loss: proceeds - disposal_costs - carrying_amount_at_disposal.
Journal preview lines link directly to disposal row.
Supersession behavior:
Event corrections create new asset_impairments/asset_disposals rows with supersedes_id.
Prior event rows remain immutable.
FX policy
Selected-rate service only; no raw provider table reads.
Default rate_mode: month_end_locked.
Allowed override: daily_selected only when tenant policy permits transaction-date basis.
Same-currency behavior: fx_rate_used=1.000000, fx_rate_date=event/depreciation date, fx_rate_source="same_currency".
Persist FX fields on all financially impacting FAR rows:
schedule: fx_rate_used, fx_rate_date, fx_rate_source.
impairment/disposal (if currency conversion applies): same trio.
Month-end lock enforcement:
Missing lock in month_end_locked mode fails run and appends failed run event (error_code=MISSING_LOCKED_RATE).
Required drillability design
Mandatory drill path:
depreciation/impairment/disposal amount
-> schedule or event row
-> asset
-> acquisition snapshot/source artifact
Required endpoints:
POST /api/v1/far/run
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/far/results/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}/assets/{asset_id}
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}/depreciation-lines/{line_id}
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}/impairments/{impairment_id}
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}/disposals/{disposal_id}
GET /api/v1/far/run/{run_id}/journal-entries/{journal_id}
Response contract:
DrillResponseBase-compatible (parent_reference_id, source_reference_id, correlation_id, deterministic child_ids).
Lineage completeness gate before terminal completion:
every schedule line resolves to asset + source artifact.
every impairment/disposal resolves to asset.
every journal entry resolves to exactly one source row.
failure appends failed event with error_code=LINEAGE_INCOMPLETE.
Required control-plane integration points
Module enablement: FAR APIs and workflow starts must check module_code="fixed_assets" enablement.
RBAC: FAR actions evaluated via control-plane evaluator (deny-over-allow).
Workflow eligibility: enforce when workflow instance/stage context is provided.
Quotas: enforce at API ingress, job submission, worker execution, export path if FAR export added.
Isolation routing: fail closed if route cannot be resolved.
Context token:
API routes require valid control-plane token with module claim match.
Workflow-triggered/internal commands validate token (or signed internal execution token) before writes.
All FAR writes remain AuditWriter-only, async SQLAlchemy only, tenant-scoped RLS runtime active.
Recommended implementation sequence
1D.5.1: FAR models + migration (far_runs, far_run_events, assets, asset_depreciation_schedule, asset_impairments, asset_disposals, asset_journal_entries) with RLS + append-only.
1D.5.2: FAR schemas (run requests, asset inputs, impairment/disposal inputs, drill responses).
1D.5.3: Service modules:
asset_registry.py
depreciation_engine.py
impairment_handler.py
disposal_handler.py
journal_builder.py
lineage_validation.py
drilldown_service.py
service_facade.py
1D.5.4: FAR Temporal workflow + activities (compact payload, idempotent stage writes).
1D.5.5: FAR API endpoints + router wiring + worker registration + control-plane guards.
1D.5.6: Tests:
unit (depreciation math, partial periods, impairment/disposal, journal linkage, lineage checks)
integration (auth/schema, workflow runtime, control-plane denial, FX policy, RLS, append-only)
deterministic full-suite run.
Recommendation
Ready for audit review.

Four tightening instructions before coding
A. Freeze the naming decision now
The design says:

module_code = "fixed_assets" (recommended) vs "far"

This must be locked before implementation.

My recommendation
Use:

module_code = "fixed_assets"
Reason:

clearer to new developers

better aligned with module registry naming

“FAR” can remain a business label, but fixed_assets is safer in code

Do not leave this open during implementation.

B. Define asset correction semantics explicitly
You said:

corrections via new rows / supersedes_id

Good, but you should explicitly define:

which asset fields can be corrected by supersession

whether correction triggers schedule regeneration

whether historical schedule rows remain visible but inactive

Recommended rule
Asset registry corrections that affect depreciation basis must trigger:

new asset row with supersedes_id

new schedule_version_token

no mutation of old schedule rows

effective version resolved from latest valid asset chain node

Lock that rule before implementation.

C. Clarify impairment/disposal interaction order
This is important.

If an asset has:

impairment first, then disposal

or disposal effective in same period as impairment

you need deterministic precedence.

Recommended rule
Order events by:

effective_date

event_type precedence if same date:

impairment first

disposal second

created_at / id as final tiebreaker

That keeps carrying amount deterministic.

D. Partial-period policy should be frozen more explicitly
You wrote:

pro-rata by day count for first/last partial month

Good, but define:

exact day-count convention

Recommended
Use:

actual days in month

from in_service_date through month-end for first period

from month-start through disposal/effective date for final period

No 30/360 assumptions in 1D.5 core.

Additional small recommendation
For asset_journal_entries, require exactly one of:

depreciation_schedule_id

impairment_id

disposal_id

Not “nullable links” loosely.

Make it a constrained one-of relationship at application validation level, and test it.

That keeps journal lineage clean.

we need WDV implemented but may be few people will use it

Good. This is exactly the kind of decision that separates a toy engine from a real CFO-grade engine.

You’re right:

“We need WDV implemented but maybe few people will use it.”

Here’s the straight answer:

If you are building AI CFO Brain, not a lightweight accounting helper,
WDV must exist in Phase 1D.5 core.

Not because everyone uses it.
But because:

Indian tax users use WDV heavily.

Some IFRS reporters use reducing balance for certain asset classes.

Many ERP migrations require WDV parity.

Without WDV, FAR looks incomplete in enterprise eyes.

So yes — we implement it.

But we implement it cleanly, deterministically, and without bloating scope.

The Correct Way to Add WDV (Without Breaking Design)
We extend depreciation methods from:

straight_line

non_depreciable

to:

straight_line

reducing_balance ← (WDV)

non_depreciable

Do NOT add:

double declining

sum of years digits

units of production

revaluation model

Keep it tight.

How WDV Should Be Designed (Governance-First)
WDV must follow deterministic rules:

1️⃣ Policy Storage
On assets table:

Add:

depreciation_method ENUM:
  straight_line
  reducing_balance
  non_depreciable

reducing_balance_rate_annual (nullable)
Rules:

required when method = reducing_balance

must be > 0

must be <= 1.000000

quantized to 6dp

2️⃣ Monthly Computation Rule
For WDV:

Annual rate → monthly rate conversion:

You must freeze this formula.

Two options:

A) Simple division
monthly_rate = annual_rate / 12

B) Effective compounding
monthly_rate = 1 - (1 - annual_rate)^(1/12)

For enterprise correctness → use effective compounding.

Otherwise accumulated rounding drift happens.

So freeze:

monthly_rate = 1 - (1 - annual_rate)^(1/12)
Quantized to 12dp internal, 6dp persisted.

3️⃣ Monthly Depreciation Formula
For each month:

depreciation = opening_carrying_amount * monthly_rate
Constraints:

carrying amount must never go below residual value

final month residual adjustment must apply deterministic anchor logic

4️⃣ Partial Period Policy (Critical)
If in-service date is mid-month:

First month:

pro-rata = monthly_depreciation * (active_days / total_days_in_month)
Where:

active_days = days from in_service_date to month_end inclusive

total_days = actual calendar days

Do NOT:

use 30/360

use approximate month fractions

Actual days only.

5️⃣ Impairment Interaction
After impairment:

New carrying amount becomes base.
Future WDV calculation must restart from:

new_carrying_amount
Same monthly_rate.
New schedule_version_token.

No retroactive rewrite.

6️⃣ Disposal Interaction
At disposal date:

Stop future schedule generation.
Compute gain/loss using carrying amount at disposal date.

No further depreciation rows.

Why WDV Is Slightly More Dangerous Than Straight-Line
WDV introduces:

compounding rounding effects

residual floor logic

impairment interaction complexity

partial month edge cases

If not deterministic, it becomes unstable.

But your platform already has:

6dp quantization

schedule_version_token

append-only rows

deterministic regeneration

Frozen Decisions

Module code (locked)
Locked value: fixed_assets
Justification: it matches existing namespace and runtime scaffolding (services/fixed_assets, FixedAssetsWorkflow, worker registration). Changing to far would create avoidable naming drift and control-plane policy duplication.
Asset correction semantics (locked)
Any correction to an asset is append-only via a new assets row with supersedes_id pointing to prior version.
Changes that mandate schedule regeneration:
capitalized_amount
capitalization_date
in_service_date
depreciation_method
useful_life_months
residual_value
asset_currency
reporting_currency
rate_mode
any impairment/disposal event that changes carrying value trajectory
Changes that do not mandate regeneration (metadata-only): descriptive fields not used in depreciation math (e.g., display description/category label), but still require superseding row.
Effective version resolution:
Supersession chain is linear (one successor per prior version).
Effective version for a run = terminal row in chain as of run acceptance timestamp.
Event ordering semantics (locked)
Processing order key per asset:
event_date ASC
same-date precedence: impairment before disposal
tie-breaker within same class/date: created_at ASC, then id ASC
Adjacent periods: strict chronological application by date.
Validation rule: disposal on date D blocks any subsequent impairment/disposal with date > D for that asset in same effective chain.
Partial-period convention (locked)
Only convention in 1D.5 core: Actual/Actual (monthly pro-rata), inclusive day count.
Formula:
partial_depr = full_month_depr * (eligible_days / days_in_month)
First partial period: from in_service_date to month-end (inclusive).
Last partial period: from month-start to disposal/end-of-life date (inclusive).
No alternative day-count basis is allowed in 1D.5.
Journal lineage one-of rule (locked)
Each FAR journal row must reference exactly one source class:
depreciation schedule row or
impairment row or
disposal row
Never multiple, never none.
Lineage fields (parent_reference_id, source_reference_id, correlation_id) must be copied from the selected source row.
B) Explicit Invariants

FAR module code is strictly fixed_assets.
FAR remains isolated from revenue/lease/prepaid/consolidation business logic.
All FAR writes are AuditWriter-only; no direct mutable updates.
assets, schedules, events, journals are append-only and tenant-RLS protected.
Supersession is new-row-only; no in-place correction.
Schedule regeneration is mandatory for any schedule-driving change.
Event application order is deterministic and stable for replays.
Partial-period depreciation uses one fixed convention only.
Journal lineage is enforced as exactly-one-source.
Terminal completion requires lineage completeness validation.
C) Implementation-Safe Confirmation

Confirmed implementation-safe.
These locks remove ambiguity in naming, version resolution, event ordering, period math, and lineage traceability, and are compatible with existing Phase 1D.1 + 1E architecture and controls.

Correct placement
Keep it here:
Module: fixed_assets

Sub-domain: depreciation_engine

Capability / feature: reducing_balance (WDV)

Do not make it:
a separate product module

a separate bounded context

a separate workflow family unless later scale demands it

Why this is the right choice
WDV is not a different business domain.
It is just another depreciation method inside FAR.

The same asset still needs:

asset registry

capitalization source

useful life / residual handling

impairment

disposal

journal preview

drillability

lineage

control-plane checks

If you split WDV into a separate module, you create unnecessary duplication for:

asset tables

journal lineage

event ordering

disposal logic

impairment logic

control-plane enforcement

That would be bad architecture.

Best design
Inside fixed_assets:

depreciation_method = straight_line

depreciation_method = reducing_balance

depreciation_method = non_depreciable

And in code:

depreciation_engine.py

straight_line.py

reducing_balance.py

shared validator / dispatcher

So it is modular inside the module, but not a separate platform module.

Recommended rollout
Because few users may need it, treat WDV as:

a feature within fixed_assets

optionally controlled by package or feature flag

So:

FAR core ships with straight-line + non-depreciable

WDV can be enabled by:

tenant package

feature flag

jurisdiction policy

That gives you flexibility without bad architecture.

Final recommendation
WDV = feature/capability inside fixed_assets, not a separate module.

Phase 1D.5 — Fixed Assets Core Implementation Prompt

fixed_assets

=======================================================
MANDATORY INVARIANTS
=======================================================

1. Fixed Assets is a separate module permanently.

=======================================================
FROZEN DESIGN CONTRACTS TO IMPLEMENT
=======================================================

A. MODULE CODE
Locked value:
fixed_assets

B. ASSET CORRECTION SEMANTICS
- Any correction to an asset is append-only via a new assets row with supersedes_id pointing to prior version.
- Changes that mandate schedule regeneration:
  - capitalized_amount
  - capitalization_date
  - in_service_date
  - depreciation_method
  - useful_life_months
  - reducing_balance_rate_annual
  - residual_value
  - asset_currency
  - reporting_currency
  - rate_mode
  - any impairment/disposal event that changes carrying value trajectory
- Metadata-only descriptive changes still require superseding asset row, but do not mandate schedule regeneration unless depreciation basis changes.
- Effective version for a run = terminal row in supersession chain as of run acceptance timestamp.

C. EVENT ORDERING SEMANTICS
Processing order per asset:
1. event_date ASC
2. same-date precedence:
   - impairment before disposal
3. tie-breaker:
   - created_at ASC
   - id ASC

Validation rule:
- disposal on date D blocks any subsequent impairment/disposal with date > D for that asset in same effective chain

D. PARTIAL-PERIOD CONVENTION
Only convention allowed in 1D.5:
Actual/Actual monthly pro-rata with inclusive day count

Formula:
partial_depr = full_month_depr * (eligible_days / days_in_month)

Rules:
- first partial period: in_service_date to month-end inclusive
- last partial period: month-start to disposal/end-of-life date inclusive
- no alternative day-count basis allowed in 1D.5

E. JOURNAL LINEAGE ONE-OF RULE
Each FAR journal row must reference exactly one source class:
- depreciation schedule row
- impairment row
- disposal row

Never multiple, never none.

=======================================================
DEPRECIATION LOGIC RULES
=======================================================

Supported methods in 1D.5 core:
- straight_line
- reducing_balance
- non_depreciable

A. STRAIGHT_LINE
- deterministic monthly schedule
- residual floor enforcement
- Actual/Actual partial-period handling
- no carrying amount below residual value
- final residual rounding drift assigned deterministically to final row of schedule_version_token

B. REDUCING_BALANCE (WDV)
- deterministic monthly reducing balance schedule
- annual rate required
- monthly rate formula is LOCKED as:
  monthly_rate = 1 - (1 - annual_rate)^(1/12)

Implementation rules:
- internal computation precision may exceed persisted precision
- persist rate values and row amounts under platform quantization policy
- monthly depreciation = opening_carrying_amount * monthly_rate
- carrying amount must never go below residual value
- first/last partial month must use Actual/Actual pro-rata against monthly depreciation
- after impairment, future schedule restarts from impaired carrying amount with new schedule_version_token
- after disposal, no future depreciation rows

C. NON_DEPRECIABLE
- no depreciation schedule rows generated
- asset remains registry-only unless impairment/disposal occurs

=======================================================
IMPAIRMENT / DISPOSAL RULES
=======================================================

A. IMPAIRMENT
- append-only event
- reduce carrying amount at event date
- regenerate future schedule prospectively with new schedule_version_token
- no retroactive mutation
- journal preview rows must trace directly to impairment row

B. DISPOSAL
- append-only event
- stop depreciation after disposal effective date
- compute deterministic gain/loss:
  proceeds - disposal_costs - carrying_amount_at_disposal
- journal preview rows must trace directly to disposal row

=======================================================
FX POLICY
=======================================================

Selected-rate service only; no raw provider table reads.

Default rate_mode:
- month_end_locked

Allowed override:
- daily_selected only when tenant policy permits transaction-date basis

Same-currency behavior:
- fx_rate_used = 1.000000
- fx_rate_date = depreciation/event date
- fx_rate_source = "same_currency"

Persist FX fields on all financially impacting FAR rows:
- depreciation schedule
- impairment events (if conversion applies)
- disposal events (if conversion applies)

Month-end lock enforcement:
- missing lock in month_end_locked mode fails run
- append failed run event with error_code = MISSING_LOCKED_RATE

=======================================================
LINEAGE + DRILLABILITY
=======================================================

Mandatory drill path:

depreciation / impairment / disposal amount
→ schedule or event row
→ asset
→ acquisition snapshot / source artifact

Implement deterministic endpoints:

POST /api/v1/fixed-assets/run
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/results/{run_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}/assets/{asset_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}/depreciation-lines/{line_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}/impairments/{impairment_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}/disposals/{disposal_id}
GET /api/v1/fixed-assets/run/{run_id}/journal-entries/{journal_id}

Rules:
- use DrillResponseBase-compatible shape
- include parent_reference_id
- include source_reference_id
- include correlation_id
- include child_ids
- pure read only
- deterministic ordering only

Lineage completeness gate before completion:
- every schedule row resolves to asset + source acquisition artifact
- every impairment/disposal resolves to asset
- every journal row resolves to exactly one source row
If incomplete:
- append failed event
- error_code = LINEAGE_INCOMPLETE

=======================================================
CONTROL-PLANE INTEGRATION
=======================================================

FAR execution must enforce:
- module enablement with module_code = fixed_assets
- RBAC
- workflow eligibility where applicable
- quota check
- isolation route resolution
- valid control-plane context token

Use module-specific token claim checks.

Identified Inconsistencies (Critical / High / Medium / Low)
CRITICAL: Revenue and Lease do not implement version-token-based regenerated schedule versions; remeasurement remains metadata/event style, not harmonized with Prepaid/FAR versioned schedule model.
Evidence: revenue/remeasurement.py:165, lease/remeasurement.py:147, no schedule token columns in revenue.py:140, lease.py:113.

CRITICAL: Revenue and Lease remeasurement idempotency is weak (no explicit idempotency_key + no strict unique constraints on modification events comparable to Prepaid/FAR).
Evidence: revenue.py:226, lease.py:180 vs prepaid/far idempotent uniques prepaid.py:169, fixed_assets.py:135.

HIGH: Prepaid journal preview includes superseded schedule versions because it reads all run schedules, not effective token only.
Evidence: prepaid/service_facade.py:372, effective-token filtering exists only in results path prepaid/service_facade.py:603.

HIGH: Lease journal one-of lineage source is not DB-enforced (both-null or both-set can exist structurally).
Evidence: nullable refs in lease.py:231, lease.py:236, and no check constraint comparable to FAR fixed_assets.py:214.

HIGH: Retry semantics can skip pending remeasurement/regeneration work due stage-level early returns when any rows already exist.
Evidence: revenue/service_facade.py:203, lease/service_facade.py:255, prepaid/service_facade.py:219, fixed_assets/service_facade.py:289.

MEDIUM: Same-date ordering in revenue/lease modifications lacks explicit tie-break hierarchy beyond date.
Evidence: revenue/remeasurement.py:55, lease/remeasurement.py:49.

MEDIUM: Supersedes chain integrity (cycle/multi-parent prevention) is not uniformly enforced in DB or shared validator across engines.
Evidence: self-FKs exist (e.g., revenue.py:72, prepaid.py:202), but no explicit cycle checks in chain resolution code.

MEDIUM: Partial-period treatment differs by engine and is not normalized through shared policy contract.
Evidence: FAR Actual/Actual pro-rata in methods straight_line.py:49, reducing_balance.py:54; Revenue straight-line month-end points revenue/schedule_generator.py:185; Lease periodic interest model lease/interest_engine.py:12.

LOW: Journal namespace usage is mostly aligned (REV/LSE/PPD/FAR mapping exists).
Evidence: journal_namespace.py:7.

Mutation Risk Assessment
No direct in-place mutation pattern found in engine service code paths (update/delete/session.add not present in audited engine services).
Append-only trigger list includes all audited engine tables.
Evidence: append_only.py:35 through append_only.py:63.
Overall mutation risk: LOW at service layer, MEDIUM at model-governance layer where supersession constraints are not structurally strict.
Supersession Risk Assessment
Revenue: supersession exists on contract/adjustment, but no schedule-version chain for remeasurement output selection; risk HIGH.
Lease: similar to revenue; risk HIGH.
Prepaid: strong version token + adjustment chain, but effective journaling not constrained to effective token; risk MEDIUM.
Fixed Assets: strongest end-to-end chain and effective-token resolution; risk LOW/MEDIUM (cycle protections still not centralized).
FX Policy Divergence Summary
Selected-rate-only invariant is respected across all engines (uses list_manual_monthly_rates / resolve_selected_rate).
Divergence 1: default rate mode differs (daily in revenue/lease vs month_end_locked in prepaid/fixed_assets).
Evidence: revenue.py:111, lease.py:99, prepaid.py:73, fixed_assets.py:68.
Divergence 2: lock-failure behavior normalized only in prepaid/fixed_assets via MISSING_LOCKED_RATE; revenue/lease emit generic validation messages.
Evidence: prepaid/schedule_generator.py:29, fixed_assets/depreciation_engine.py:30, revenue/schedule_generator.py:95, lease/liability_schedule.py:81.
Error Code Normalization Recommendation
Current emitted patterns are mixed:
Explicit code class: MISSING_LOCKED_RATE (prepaid/fixed_assets).
Message-based only: "LINEAGE_INCOMPLETE" raised via ValidationError message in facades (revenue/service_facade.py:420, lease/service_facade.py:700, prepaid/service_facade.py:458, fixed_assets/service_facade.py:689).
Base error remains validation_error unless custom subclass sets code (exceptions.py:46).
Recommendation outcome: define a unified accounting error namespace and apply same code semantics for equivalent failure classes across all four engines.
Deterministic Replay Risk Summary
Strong deterministic replay posture: Prepaid/FAR (tokenized versions + deterministic sorting + idempotent unique keys).
Weak replay posture: Revenue/Lease due no schedule-version chain and weaker modification idempotency contracts.
Cross-engine replay hazard: stage early-return short-circuit can leave partially materialized runs unreconciled after interruption (if transaction boundaries are not fully atomic per activity).
Recommendation
Harmonization pass required before next phase.

🚨 You Cannot Move Forward Yet
You must do 1D.6 enforcement.

Why?

Because right now:

Prepaid & FAR are version-token deterministic engines.

Revenue & Lease are still “event-based remeasurement” engines.

That means:

You have two architectural philosophies co-existing.

That is dangerous.

🔴 The Two Critical Problems
1️⃣ Revenue & Lease Lack Versioned Schedule Regeneration
This is not cosmetic.

Right now:

Prepaid/FAR → regenerate forward schedules with new schedule_version_token

Revenue/Lease → record adjustment rows without materializing regenerated schedule versions

That means:

Effective version resolution is inconsistent

Journal preview logic is inconsistent

Replay determinism differs

Supersession logic is incomplete

This is the single biggest architectural fracture.

2️⃣ Early-Return Stage Short-Circuit
This is subtle but dangerous.

If stage logic says:

“If schedule rows already exist, skip regeneration”

You have:

Retry instability

Partial-run survivability risk

Inconsistent recovery after crash

Replay inconsistency

This must be removed.

Deterministic engines cannot depend on “row exists” checks.

🔥 Required 1D.6 Enforcement Scope
You are not doing light cleanup.

You are doing structural harmonization.

Phase 1D.6 — Enforcement Plan
🔧 6A — Revenue & Lease Version Token Refactor (CRITICAL)
Revenue and Lease must:

Introduce schedule_version_token

Regenerate forward schedules on remeasurement

Never update existing schedule rows

Insert new rows under new version token

Use unique constraints identical to Prepaid/FAR

Journal only effective version

Idempotency enforced via token

This is mandatory.

No half-measures.

🔧 6B — Remove Early-Return Stage Logic
Across:

revenue

lease

prepaid

fixed_assets

Remove:

if rows_exist:
    return
Replace with:

deterministic idempotent regeneration

safe upsert logic based on unique constraints

no control flow shortcuts

🔧 6C — Journal Filtering Alignment
Prepaid must filter to effective version before journaling (like FAR already does).

Revenue/Lease must:

Only journal effective schedule version

Never re-journal superseded rows

🔧 6D — Error Code Namespace Harmonization
Define canonical error codes:

MISSING_LOCKED_RATE
LINEAGE_INCOMPLETE
INVALID_EVENT_SEQUENCE
VERSION_CHAIN_BROKEN
DUPLICATE_IDEMPOTENT_REQUEST
All engines must use structured error codes, not free-form ValidationError messages.

🔧 6E — Supersession Chain Hardening
Add:

centralized chain validation

cycle detection

multi-parent prevention

same-tenant enforcement

Make this reusable utility in accounting_common.

🔧 6F — FX Default Policy Alignment
Right now:

Revenue/Lease default daily

Prepaid/FAR default month_end_locked

Pick one policy strategy and document difference intentionally.

My recommendation:

Keep business defaults different if domain-driven,
but unify lock failure behavior and error codes.

🎯 What This Achieves
After 1D.6:

All engines will have:

Same regeneration semantics

Same supersession behavior

Same version resolution logic

Same journaling policy

Same failure semantics

Same replay determinism

Then MIS layer can trust engine outputs.

architectural decisions implemented
Revenue and Lease now use explicit schedule_version_token-based forward regeneration and never update schedule rows in place.
Journal preview paths in Revenue and Lease now read only effective schedule versions (superseded versions excluded).
Shared supersession-chain enforcement added in accounting_common (cycle detection, branching detection, same-tenant enforcement, terminal resolution).
Unified accounting error codes enforced via shared constants + AccountingValidationError.
Missing-locked-rate behavior aligned to shared MISSING_LOCKED_RATE error semantics in Prepaid and Fixed Assets.
Migration 0011 hardened and replay-safe with static Alembic operations; revision id shortened to fit alembic_version.version_num constraint.
refactor summary per engine
Revenue:
Added version-token/idempotent remeasurement flow.
Added effective-version journal filtering.
Added duplicate-idempotent conflict validation.
Lease:
Added version-token/idempotent modification flow for liability/ROU schedules.
Added effective-version journal filtering.
Enforced exactly-one-source journal lineage constraint.
Prepaid:
Hardened adjustment replay/idempotency to avoid chain corruption on re-run.
Aligned missing locked-rate exception to unified accounting error contract.
Fixed Assets:
Aligned missing locked-rate exception to unified accounting error contract.
Aligned disposal/event-order violations to unified INVALID_EVENT_SEQUENCE semantics.
Cross-engine:
Removed stage-level short-circuit behavior in orchestration paths where rows already exist; replay now relies on deterministic idempotent inserts + uniqueness.
